2
Let x(q) be the second derivative of q**3/6 - 13*q**2 - 17*q. Let s be x(16). What is the units digit of (s - 0)*(-7)/2?
5
Suppose -4*q + 4*c - 12 = 2*c, c + 29 = -5*q. Let n(d) = -d**3 - 3*d**2 + d + 9. What is the tens digit of n(q)?
5

3

1

1
